Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 116 (the Apollo 12 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Ron Burkey, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 116 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-071
	19:09 AUG. 11,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

016440,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016441,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016442,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 116.
016443,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM) 
016444,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 12.
016445,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
016446,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
016447,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
016448,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
016449,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 391-473
016450,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
016451,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.

016453,000015:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2017-01-22 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.

Page 391 

016468,000030:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016469,000031:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016470,000032:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016471,000033:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016472,000034: 
016473,000035:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016474,000036: 
016475,000037:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016476,000038:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016477,000039:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016478,000040:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016479,000041: 
016480,000042:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016481,000043:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016482,000044:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016483,000045:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016484,000046:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016485,000047: 
016486,000048:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016487,000049:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016488,000050:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016489,000051:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016490,000052: 
016491,000053:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016492,000054:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016493,000055: 
016494,000056:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016495,000057: 
016496,000058:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016497,000059:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016498,000060:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016499,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016500,000062:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016501,000063: 
016502,000064:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016503,000065:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016504,000066:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016505,000067:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016506,000068: 
016507,000069:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016508,000070:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016509,000071:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016510,000072:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016511,000073:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016512,000074: 
016513,000075:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016514,000076: 
016515,000077:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016516,000078:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016517,000079:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 392 

016519,000081:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016520,000082:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016521,000083:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016522,000084:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016523,000085:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016524,000086:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016525,000087:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016526,000088:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016527,000089:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016528,000090:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016529,000091: 
016530,000092:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016531,000093:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016532,000094:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016533,000095: 
016534,000096:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016535,000097: 
016536,000098:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016537,000099:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016538,000100:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016539,000101: 
016540,000102:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016541,000103:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016542,000104:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016543,000105:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016544,000106:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016545,000107:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016546,000108:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016547,000109: 
016548,000110:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016549,000111:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016550,000112: 
016551,000113:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016552,000114: 
016553,000115:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016554,000116:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016555,000117:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016556,000118:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016557,000119: 
016558,000120:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016559,000121: 
016560,000122:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016561,000123:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016562,000124:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016563,000125:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016564,000126: 
016565,000127:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 393 

016567,000129:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016568,000130: 
016569,000131:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016570,000132: 
016571,000133:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016572,000134:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016573,000135: 
016574,000136:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016575,000137:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016576,000138:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016577,000139:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016578,000140: 
016579,000141:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016580,000142:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016581,000143: 
016582,000144:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016583,000145:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016584,000146:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016585,000147:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016586,000148: 
016587,000149:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016588,000150:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016589,000151: 
016590,000152:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016591,000153:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016592,000154: 
016593,000155:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016594,000156: 
016595,000157:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016596,000158:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016597,000159:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016598,000160:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016599,000161: 
016600,000162:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016601,000163:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016602,000164: 
016603,000165:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016604,000166:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016605,000167: 
016606,000168:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016607,000169:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016608,000170:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016609,000171: 
016610,000172:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016611,000173: 
016612,000174:                                                                                                  #  ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016613,000175:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 394 

016615,000177:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016616,000178:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016617,000179: 
016618,000180:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016619,000181: 
016620,000182:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016621,000183: 
016622,000184:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016623,000185:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016624,000186:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
016625,000187:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016626,000188:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016627,000189:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016628,000190:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016629,000191:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016630,000192:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016631,000193:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016632,000194:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016633,000195:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016634,000196:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016635,000197:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016636,000198:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
016637,000199:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016638,000200:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016639,000201:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016640,000202:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016641,000203:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016642,000204:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016643,000205:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016644,000206:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
016645,000207:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016646,000208:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13, C RELAYS
016647,000209:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016648,000210:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016649,000211:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016650,000212:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016651,000213:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016652,000214:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016653,000215:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016654,000216:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016655,000217:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016656,000218:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016657,000219: 
016658,000220:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016659,000221: 
016660,000222:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016661,000223:

016664,000226:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
016665,000227:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
016666,000228:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET      =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
016667,000229: 
016668,000230:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
016669,000231:                                                                                                  #  WDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
016670,000232:                                                                                                  #  DECRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
016671,000233:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG      =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
016672,000234: 
016673,000235:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET      =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
016674,000236:                                                                                                  #  CHAR          =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
016675,000237:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT         =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
016676,000238:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT       =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
016677,000239: 
016678,000240:                                                                                                  #  SGNON         =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
016679,000241:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM       =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
016680,000242:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
016681,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
016682,000244: 
016683,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
016684,000246:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
016685,000247:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016686,000248:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016687,000249:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016688,000250:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
016689,000251:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016690,000252:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
016691,000253:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMIN+1.
016692,000254:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016693,000255:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
016694,000256: 
016695,000257:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
016696,000258: 
016697,000259:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET        =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
016698,000260: 
016699,000261:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT         =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
016700,000262:                                                                                                  #  INREL         =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X, Y, Z, REG)
016701,000263: 
016702,000264:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM      =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
016703,000265:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR         =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN

016716,000278:                                                                                                  #  TEM4          ERASE                   EXEC TEMP

016726,000288: 
016727,000289:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016728,000290:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016729,000291:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016730,000292:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016731,000293:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016732,000294:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
016733,000295:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016734,000296:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
016735,000297:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016736,000298: 
016737,000299:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016738,000300: 
016739,000301:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016740,000302: 
016741,000303:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016742,000304:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016743,000305:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016744,000306:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016745,000307:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016746,000308:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016747,000309: 
016748,000310:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016749,000311: 
016750,000312:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT        ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016751,000313:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK        ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016752,000314:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016753,000315:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016754,000316:

016761,000323:

Page 397 

016763,000325:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016764,000326:                                                                                                  #  0             10000
016765,000327:                                                                                                  #  1             00001
016766,000328:                                                                                                  #  9             01001
016767,000329:                                                                                                  #  VERB          10001
016768,000330:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES     10010
016769,000331:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE      11001
016770,000332:                                                                                                  #  +             11010
016771,000333:                                                                                                  #  -             11011
016772,000334:                                                                                                  #  ENTER         11100
016773,000335:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR         11110
016774,000336:                                                                                                  #  NOUN          11111
016775,000337: 
016776,000338:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016777,000339:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016778,000340:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016779,000341:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016780,000342:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016781,000343:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016782,000344: 
016783,000345:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016784,000346:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016785,000347:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016786,000348:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016787,000349:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016788,000350:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016789,000351: 
016790,000352:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016791,000353: 
016792,000354:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016793,000355:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016794,000356:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016795,000357:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016796,000358:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016797,000359:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016798,000360:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016799,000361:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016800,000362:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016801,000363:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016802,000364:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016803,000365: 
016804,000366:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016805,000367: 
016806,000368:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016807,000369:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016808,000370:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016809,000371:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016810,000372:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016811,000373:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 398 

016813,000375:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016814,000376:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016815,000377:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016816,000378:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016817,000379:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016818,000380:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016819,000381:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016820,000382:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD

017242,000804:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION. HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
017243,000805:                                                                                                  #  DATA. THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0,- FOR HIGHER
017244,000806:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
017245,000807: 
017246,000808:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
017247,000809:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
017248,000810:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

017533,001095:

Page 414 

017535,001097:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
017536,001098:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017537,001099:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017538,001100:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
017539,001101:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017540,001102:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017541,001103: 
017542,001104:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017543,001105:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017544,001106: 
017545,001107:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017546,001108: 
017547,001109:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017548,001110:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017549,001111:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017550,001112: 
017551,001113:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017552,001114:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017553,001115:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017554,001116:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017555,001117:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017556,001118:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017557,001119: 
017558,001120:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017559,001121:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017560,001122:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017561,001123:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017562,001124:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017563,001125: 
017564,001126:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017565,001127:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017566,001128:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017567,001129:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017568,001130:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017569,001131:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017570,001132:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017571,001133:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017572,001134: 
017573,001135:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017574,001136:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017575,001137:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017576,001138: 
017577,001139:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017578,001140:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017579,001141: 
017580,001142:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017581,001143:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017582,001144:

Page 415 

017584,001146:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017585,001147:

018135,001697:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018136,001698:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018137,001699:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO .  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018138,001700:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018139,001701:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

018163,001725:                                                                                                  #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
018164,001726:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE  OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY  1) DECIMAL MACHINE
018165,001727:                                                                                                  #  CADR  2) MIXTURE OF OCTAL/DECIMAL DATA  3) OCTAL DATA INTO DECIMAL

018730,002292:

Page 439 

018732,002294:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018733,002295:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018734,002296:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018735,002297:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018736,002298:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018737,002299: 
018738,002300:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018739,002301:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018740,002302:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018741,002303:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018742,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018743,002305:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018744,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018745,002307: 
018746,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018747,002309:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018748,002310:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018749,002311: 
018750,002312:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018751,002313:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018752,002314: 
018753,002315:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018754,002316:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018755,002317: 
018756,002318:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018881,002443:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018882,002444:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018883,002445:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018884,002446:                                                                                                  #  
018885,002447:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018886,002448: 
018887,002449:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018888,002450:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018889,002451:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018890,002452: 
018891,002453:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018892,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018893,002455:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018894,002456: 
018895,002457: 41,3361           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018896,002458: 41,3362           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018897,002459: 41,3363           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018898,002460: 41,3364           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018899,002461: 41,3365           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018900,002462: 41,3366           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018901,002463: 41,3367           03371                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018902,002464: 41,3370           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB
