Page 452 

019325,002887: 
019326,002888:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019327,002889: 
019328,002890:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019329,002891: 
019330,002892:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019331,002893:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019332,002894:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019333,002895:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019334,002896: 
019335,002897:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019336,002898:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019337,002899:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019338,002900: 
019339,002901:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019340,002902:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019341,002903:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019342,002904:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019343,002905:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019344,002906:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019345,002907:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019346,002908:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019347,002909:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019348,002910:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019349,002911:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019350,002912: 
019351,002913: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019352,002914: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019353,002915: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019354,002916: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019355,002917: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019356,002918: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019357,002919: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019358,002920: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019359,002921: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019360,002922: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019361,002923: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019362,002924: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019363,002925: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019364,002926: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019365,002927: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019366,002928: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019367,002929: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019368,002930: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019369,002931: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019370,002932: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019371,002933: 
019372,002934: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019373,002935:

Page 453 

019375,002937:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019376,002938:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019377,002939:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019378,002940:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019379,002941:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019380,002942: 
019381,002943:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019382,002944:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019383,002945:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019384,002946: 
019385,002947:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019386,002948:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019387,002949: 
019388,002950:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019389,002951:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019390,002952:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019391,002953:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019392,002954:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019393,002955: 
019394,002956:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019395,002957:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019396,002958:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019397,002959:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019398,002960: 
019399,002961:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019400,002962:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019401,002963:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019402,002964:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019403,002965:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019404,002966:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019405,002967:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019406,002968: 
019407,002969:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019408,002970:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019409,002971: 
019410,002972:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019411,002973:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019412,002974: 
019413,002975:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019414,002976:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019415,002977: 
019416,002978:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019417,002979:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019418,002980:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019419,002981:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019420,002982:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019421,002983:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019422,002984:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019423,002985: 
019424,002986:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 454 

019426,002988:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019427,002989:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019428,002990:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019429,002991:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019430,002992:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019431,002993:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019432,002994:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019433,002995:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019434,002996:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019435,002997: 
019436,002998:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019437,002999:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019438,003000: 
019439,003001:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019440,003002: 
019441,003003:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019442,003004:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019443,003005:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
019444,003006:    4156           34736                           CAF      BIT14

019545,003107:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).

019548,003110:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019549,003111:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019550,003112:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019551,003113:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019552,003114:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019553,003115:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019554,003116: 
019555,003117:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019556,003118:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019557,003119:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019558,003120:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019559,003121:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019560,003122: 
019561,003123:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019562,003124:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019563,003125:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019564,003126:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019565,003127:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019566,003128:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019567,003129:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019568,003130:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019569,003131:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019570,003132:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019571,003133: 
019572,003134:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 457 

019574,003136:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019575,003137:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019576,003138:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019577,003139:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019578,003140:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019579,003141: 
019580,003142:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019581,003143:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019582,003144:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019583,003145:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019584,003146:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019585,003147:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019586,003148:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019587,003149:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019588,003150: 
019589,003151:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019590,003152: 
019591,003153:    4220           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.

Page 465 

019917,003479:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019918,003480: 
019919,003481:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019920,003482:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019921,003483:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019922,003484:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019923,003485: 
019924,003486:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019925,003487:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019926,003488:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019927,003489:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019928,003490:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019929,003491:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019930,003492:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019931,003493: 
019932,003494:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019933,003495:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019934,003496:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019935,003497:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019936,003498:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019937,003499: 
019938,003500:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019939,003501:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019940,003502:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019941,003503:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019942,003504:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019943,003505: 
019944,003506:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019945,003507:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019946,003508:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019947,003509: 
019948,003510: 
019949,003511:                                                                                                  #  .
019950,003512: 
019951,003513:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019952,003514:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019953,003515:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019954,003516:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019955,003517: 
019956,003518:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019957,003519:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019958,003520:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019959,003521:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019960,003522:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019961,003523:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 466 

019963,003525:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019964,003526: 
019965,003527:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019966,003528:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019967,003529:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019968,003530:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019969,003531:    4443           10631                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019970,003532:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019971,003533: 
019972,003534:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019973,003535:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019974,003536: 
019975,003537: 04,2631                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019976,003538: 04,2631                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019977,003539: 04,2631           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019978,003540: 04,2632           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019979,003541: 04,2633           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019980,003542: 04,2634           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019981,003543: 04,2635           30001                           CA       L                                     
019982,003544: 04,2636           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019983,003545: 04,2637           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019984,003546: 
019985,003547:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019986,003548:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019987,003549:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019988,003550:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019989,003551:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019990,003552: 
019991,003553:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019992,003554:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019993,003555:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019994,003556:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019995,003557:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019996,003558:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019997,003559:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019998,003560:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019999,003561:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
020000,003562:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
020001,003563:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.

020157,003719:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020158,003720:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020159,003721:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020160,003722:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020161,003723:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020162,003724:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020163,003725:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
